TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE	
[Part  II—Sec. 2
NOTIFICATIONS BY GOVERNMENT
HOME DEPARTMENT
Consent under section 6 of Delhi Special Police 
Establishment  Act
[G.O. Ms. No. 46, Home (Citizenship-II) 27th January 2022,  
¬î 14, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HO/86/2022.—Under section 6 of the Delhi 
Special Police Establishment Act, 1946 (Central Act 25 of 
1946), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby accords his consent 
to the members of the Delhi Special Police Establishment 
to exercise their powers and jurisdiction in the whole of 
the State of Tamil Nadu to investigate the case registered 
in Chengalpet District, Palur Police Station Crime Nos. 408 
and 421 of 2021 for the offences under sections 420, 468, 
471, 224, 511, and 224 @ 224, 120(B), 109 respectively of 
the Indian Penal Code (Central Act XLV of 1860).
	
	
	
       S.K. PRABAKAR,
	
	
    Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

REVENUE AND DISASTER MANAGEMENT 
DEPARTMENT
Demarcation of Containment Zones to control COVID-19 - 
List of Containment Zones as on 21.01.2022 under the 
Disaster Management Act, 2005.
[G.O. Ms. No. 50, Revenue and Disaster Management (DM-4) 
27th January 2022, ¬î 14, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´- 
2053.]
No.II(2)/REVDM/90/2022.—The list of Containment Zones 
as on 21.01.2022 is notified under Disaster Management 
Act, 2005 for Demarcation of Containment zone to control 
Corona Virus.
